2021-10-20 13:55:59.849903 ==> start try [update class] 
select r.id, RTRIM(g.name) + ' - ' + rtrim(ju.name) as 'Группа - наставник', d.name as 'День недели' , 
                    k.name as 'Кабинет', r.tstart as 'Начало', r.tend as 'Окончание', 
                    jc.acchour as 'Акк. час', jc.hday as 'Занятий в день', r.comment as 'Доп. информация', 
                    r.idGroups as 'Группа', d.id as 'День'
                from rasp r
                join kabs k on r.idKabs = k.id
                join days d on r.idDays = d.id
                join groups g on r.idGroups = g.id
                join (select gu.id, u.name from groups gu join users u on gu.idUsers = u.id) ju on ju.id = g.id
                join (select cu.id, cu.acchour, cu.hday from courses cu) jc on jc.id = g.idCourses  order by d.id, k.id, r.tstart

                    k.name as 'Кабинет', r.tstart as 'Начало', r.tend as 'Окончание',

select r.id, RTRIM(g.name) + ' - ' + rtrim(ju.name) as 'Группа - наставник', d.name as 'День недели' , 
                    k.name as 'Кабинет', r.tstart as 'Начало', r.tend as 'Окончание', 
                    jc.acchour as 'Акк. час', jc.hday as 'Занятий в день', r.comment as 'Доп. информация', 
                    r.idGroups as 'Группа', d.id as 'День'
                from rasp r
                join kabs k on r.idKabs = k.id
                join days d on r.idDays = d.id
                join groups g on r.idGroups = g.id
                join (select gu.id, u.name from groups gu join users u on gu.idUsers = u.id) ju on ju.id = g.id
                join (select cu.id, cu.acchour, cu.hday from courses cu) jc on jc.id = g.idCourses where g.idUsers = 15 order by d.id, k.id, r.tstart

select r.id, RTRIM(g.name) + ' - ' + rtrim(ju.name) as 'Группа - наставник', d.name as 'День недели' , 
                    k.name as 'Кабинет', r.tstart as 'Начало', r.tend as 'Окончание', 
                    jc.acchour as 'Акк. час', jc.hday as 'Занятий в день', r.comment as 'Доп. информация', 
                    r.idGroups as 'Группа', d.id as 'День'
                from rasp r

                join groups g on r.idGroups = g.id
                join (select gu.id, u.name from groups gu join users u on gu.idUsers = u.id) ju on ju.id = g.id
                join (select cu.id, cu.acchour, cu.hday from courses cu) jc on jc.id = g.idCourses where g.idUsers = 15 order by d.id, k.id, r.tstart

select r.id, RTRIM(g.name) + ' - ' + rtrim(ju.name) as 'Группа - наставник', d.name as 'День недели' , 
                    k.name as 'Кабинет', r.tstart as 'Начало', r.tend as 'Окончание', 
                    jc.acchour as 'Акк. час', jc.hday as 'Занятий в день', r.comment as 'Доп. информация', 
                    r.idGroups as 'Группа', d.id as 'День'
                from rasp r
                join kabs k on r.idKabs = k.id
                join days d on r.idDays = d.id
                join groups g on r.idGroups = g.id
                join (select gu.id, u.name from groups gu join users u on gu.idUsers = u.id) ju on ju.id = g.id

select r.id, RTRIM(g.name) + ' - ' + rtrim(ju.name) as 'Группа - наставник', d.name as 'День недели' , 
                    k.name as 'Кабинет', r.tstart as 'Начало', r.tend as 'Окончание', 
                    jc.acchour as 'Акк. час', jc.hday as 'Занятий в день', r.comment as 'Доп. информация', 
                    r.idGroups as 'Группа', d.id as 'День'
                from rasp r
                join kabs k on r.idKabs = k.id
                join days d on r.idDays = d.id
                join groups g on r.idGroups = g.id
                join (select gu.id, u.name from groups gu join users u on gu.idUsers = u.id) ju on ju.id = g.id
                join (select cu.id, cu.acchour, cu.hday from courses cu) jc on jc.id = g.idCourses where g.idUsers = 15 order by d.id, k.id, r.tstart

select r.id, RTRIM(g.name) + ' - ' + rtrim(ju.name) as 'Группа - наставник', d.name as 'День недели' , 
                    k.name as 'Кабинет', r.tstart as 'Начало', r.tend as 'Окончание', 
                    jc.acchour as 'Акк. час', jc.hday as 'Занятий в день', r.comment as 'Доп. информация', 
                    r.idGroups as 'Группа', d.id as 'День'
                from rasp r
                join kabs k on r.idKabs = k.id
                join days d on r.idDays = d.id
                join groups g on r.idGroups = g.id
                join (select gu.id, u.name from groups gu join users u on gu.idUsers = u.id) ju on ju.id = g.id
                join (select cu.id, cu.acchour, cu.hday from courses cu) jc on jc.id = g.idCourses where g.idUsers = 15 order by d.id, k.id, r.tstart

select r.id, RTRIM(g.name) + ' - ' + rtrim(ju.name) as 'Группа - наставник', d.name as 'День недели' , 
                    k.name as 'Кабинет', r.tstart as 'Начало', r.tend as 'Окончание', 
                    jc.acchour as 'Акк. час', jc.hday as 'Занятий в день', r.comment as 'Доп. информация', 
                    r.idGroups as 'Группа', d.id as 'День'
                from rasp r
                join kabs k on r.idKabs = k.id
                join days d on r.idDays = d.id
                join groups g on r.idGroups = g.id
                join (select gu.id, u.name from groups gu join users u on gu.idUsers = u.id) ju on ju.id = g.id
                join (select cu.id, cu.acchour, cu.hday from courses cu) jc on jc.id = g.idCourses where g.idUsers = 15 order by d.id, k.id, r.tstart

select r.id, RTRIM(g.name) + ' - ' + rtrim(ju.name) as 'Группа - наставник', d.name as 'День недели' , 
                    k.name as 'Кабинет', r.tstart as 'Начало', r.tend as 'Окончание', 
                    jc.acchour as 'Акк. час', jc.hday as 'Занятий в день', r.comment as 'Доп. информация', 
                    r.idGroups as 'Группа', d.id as 'День'
                from rasp r
                join kabs k on r.idKabs = k.id
                join days d on r.idDays = d.id
                join groups g on r.idGroups = g.id
                join (select gu.id, u.name from groups gu join users u on gu.idUsers = u.id) ju on ju.id = g.id
                join (select cu.id, cu.acchour, cu.hday from courses cu) jc on jc.id = g.idCourses where g.idUsers = 15 order by d.id, k.id, r.tstart
